#  [](/thread/86476-5-min-keltner-system)5 Min Keltner System 

  * 

  * [#1](/thread/86476-5-min-keltner-system "Post Permalink")

  * First Post: May 15, 2008 12:17am  May 15, 2008 12:17am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi  
  
I want to share my Futures trading system with you,Ive had so much help from this BB I thought it about time I shared some thing of mine.I trade EOD on Forex and have posted the results under the ‘trading journal’   
  
I have been day trading US Futures for 5 years and thought Id migrate over to the big boys  
  
This system works very well on Futures mainly Russell 2000 I personally use it on 1min time frame. Please make note though this is not a system that only takes 2 trades a day ,this is a scalping system designed to rack up the points. When I trade it with ER2 I stop for the day at +$500 per contract traded.  
  
On Forex it could be 20 –30 pips its up to you…but the aim is to consistently make money not sit in front of a PC all day.  
  
I’m not sure how well it will lend itself to Forex but I think for a start it has to be used on a 5min time frame.  
  
It can give as many as 30 signals a day for the whole session, the main advantage of this is……….. if you work shifts or odd hours you know you can still make some profit as signals will still be triggering. No need to upset the wife and let the tea go cold any more !  
  
The system is simple to trade although on er2 I trade with a 1 tick spread with 3 pips on Forex I will have to adjust. I’m hoping by trading it I can make any changes needed along the way.  
  
I will include my template at the end of this and the Keltner indictor but it essentially uses 2 indicators and I use it on £$  
  
The system is simple on the eye and uses 1 time frame  
  
**Keltner bands**  
  
  
Length 10  
Times ATR 1  
  
**Stochastic**  
  
  
15.3.2Use signal line only ..Colour main line to ‘none’  
15.3.3Set line at 80 and 20  
  
**Long signal**  
  
  
Price closes below the bottom K line Stochastic below 20   
Go long on the next up bar as long as stochastic still below 20   
  
**Exit**  
  
  
Move stop to break even if price touches middle K line (white)  
Take profit if price touches top band line, again it flexible and up to you  
  
**Stops**  
  
  
Up to you… if going long it can be the low of the entry candle  
Or any number of pips you prefer.  
  
Visa versa for shorts.  
  
Here is a screen shot of today up to time of posting on £$ 5min  
  
In my Futures trading platform it is fully coded and traded through Interactive Brokers TWS via Ninja Trader .It could be traded through an EA but I cant code so for me its manual atm.  
  
I don’t mind changing or adapting the system .To me if you don’t adapt or change with the markets you Die.

  * [ ExpatXXXX](expatxxxx)

  * | Membership Revoked  | Joined Feb 2008 | [540 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=60281)

Interesting system. I trade a variable of the same. Trade only Eur/Usd on the 5m tf. Utilize Stochastic set at 5-3-3, ADX set at 4, a 2sma and 5 sma with a weighted close. Trade from 5 - 11 a.m. pst and average about 10 trades per session with good results (90%). Look to take three (3) pips of net profit and trade 8 contracts per trade. Has been very consistant and profitable for the past eight months. Currently indure a 2 pip spread and have had very little difficulty. Can obtain confirmation by dropping down to 1m tf to time entry and exit. Never trade during "red" news announcements. Thanks for sharing. Keith 

All that is needed for evil to triumph is for good men to do nothing !!

  * [#8](/thread/post/2000639#post2000639 "Post Permalink")

  * May 15, 2008 2:07am  May 15, 2008 2:07am 

  * [ ExpatXXXX](expatxxxx)

  * | Membership Revoked  | Joined Feb 2008 | [540 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=60281)

Sure. I utilize a 6 pip MENTAL stop loss with my broker. For example, if I initiate a buy order at 1.5000, my stop loss is at 1.4996. (Buy at 1.5000 + 2 pip spread = 1.5002 buy point. Subtract 6 pip stop loss + 1.4996. Opposite is true of sell order. Sell at 1.5000 + 2 pip spread = sell order at 1.4998. Subtract 6 pip stop loss will be set at 1.5004. Hope that makes sense. Can review a perfect sell of Eur/ Usd recently at just five minutes ago on any chart on the 5m tf.

Appreciate all thought and critiques of my method, am never in a trade very long though. Always have my finger on the close the position trigger and NEVER walk away from the screen while in a trade. Six hours per day is not such a grind compared to many, many less rewarding careers. It is my opinion that you simply must be willing to do Some time at work in order to get paid.

I simply do not have the inclination to try to trade the news at all and am not patient enough to trade of the higher tf's than the 5 and 1m exclusively as I am obviously a scalper by nature.   * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

here the 15min chart..the sigs look good although one of the reasons for this type of system is so that you can come to the PC in an hours window and grab some points.  
  
If you want to sit and watch for the bigger moves then the 15min is the way to go..  
  
BTW on futures I bring the stop to break even when we hit the middle ma line also if I have a signal that close on or within a couple pips of the line its regarded as a none signal...   
  
Ive had $500 per contract on er2 many a time and stayed on to trade the whole session only to close up $700 per contract or up $200 per contract.. I try to get the average..if volatilty picks up and the $500 is getting easily hit time and time again quickly with good moves and signal then I increase the daily tgt  
  
I should say that on Futures I trade in pairs of contract close one at +2 ( $200) and the other at +3 ( $300) when i re read my post it says per contract.  
  
If after several trades im sitting at +4 for example and i get a signal i close both at 1/2 point profit and walk with 1 full point as its made my 5  
  
heres the 15min chart

  * May 15, 2008 4:10am  May 15, 2008 4:10am 

  * [ ExpatXXXX](expatxxxx)

  * | Membership Revoked  | Joined Feb 2008 | [540 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=60281)

Sorry folks, will try to answer as best I can. Will also check on starting a thread as I have never broached that possibility. As stated earlier, I trade daily so will work on this thread thing this afternoon. Entry signals are pretty straight forward. 2 sma should be approching or crossing 5 sma, stochastics rising above or below the 20 / 80 settings normal to this indicator and ADX should also be converging or crossing. I go with the current candle on the 5m tf and also have the 1m tf chart on the screen in order to confirm direction. The 1m chart will normally show the move 2 - 3 minutes ahead of the 5m chart. I will also try to learn about posting to actual screen shots of varios trades as this thread progresses and I figure out how to do so. It is, however, very easy to set up the indicators and back test this system at your convienence. I fully realixe that the indicators in use are lagging in nature, however, ALL indicators are lagging aren't they. You simply must be able to develope a feel for the pair you have chosen and this particular pair moves with decent volatility and yet does not move too violently. Hope this helps. Lastly, you can also trade the 1m tf with these same indicators, however, the results will be many more trades with around 70% winners. It seems, at least to me, that staying around 90% (5m tf) is good enough for the time being. I am very adaptable though and not adverse to ideas that can enhance results. 

All that is needed for evil to triumph is for good men to do nothing !!

bazuk  
  
here is one of my Futures trading charts its on a site called chart hub..my future trading platform is IRT by linnsoft and chart hub is the way we can post to let others see our chart  
  
<http://www.charthub.com/images/2008/03/14/K_chart_3>  
  
and later in the day  
  
<http://www.charthub.com/images/2008/03/14/K_chart_13>  
  
and another on this day I stopped at +5 ( $500 per contract) but the system was on 17.1 ( $1,710 per contract)  
  
<http://www.charthub.com/images/2008/04/17/System_1_5>  
  
  
  
If you go to chart hub and look for more charts from this user you will se all my charts and exploits in ER2 trading..the +39 refers to 39 points x $100 per contract so $3,900 per contract.  
  
The strike rate wasn't particularly high on winners because as you can see I cut my losers out fast..hence the 0+0 but all done in a mechanical way..I don't do emotions.the arrows you see are automatically put thier by the software as I coded it.  
  
I later changed the zero zero on both contracts and moved to a diff type of stop which turned some of those break evens into winners.. this made it easier for me to hit my 5 point tgt.  
  
Hope that helps  
  
Paulus

  * [#33](/thread/post/2001239#post2001239 "Post Permalink")

  * May 15, 2008 7:41am  May 15, 2008 7:41am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi Book times..  
  
The entry candle is where the red arrow is and i enter in the last 10secs of that arrow.by the very nature of the system my trade will always be in the opposite direction to the Keltner.  
  
I do not wait for any thing ..I don't wait for ma's to change colour or stochastic to cross..If the price is out side the channel and the stoch is OB or OS I want in and will do it on the down candle for a short up candle for a long.  
  
You will have losing trades but if their nipped in the bud you'll be ok.  
  
I think like a sparrow I come down to the lawn and take loads of little pieces of bread rather than the loaf like the wood pigeon ..if he drops it he loses the lot and may have to wait a day for another loaf to appear..I just nip down and take another small piece ..lols  
  
sorry it was the best I could think of .... ;-)  
  
  
  
Its mainly counter trend trading but I do get signals if there is a strong pull back in an uptrend for example and the price comes down through the bottom K line then I'm normally long ready for the next rally as the stoch will be over sold ...all i need is an up bar  
  
cheers  
  
Paulus

Emacro  
  
Yes tried trading it with IB ..trouble;e is if you use thier TWS as a data feed which I did it only gives you around 8 swaps and its not a smooth process getting it into IRT..  
  
In the end I moved over to MT for my Forex ..Commission is negligible really $2 round trip and ER2 and thats for a contract thats $100 per point so if you close with just 1tick ($10) you easily cover the spread  
  
I did look at Esignal but to be quite honest I really wanted a plateform I could trade through not along side ...my only other option is trade station which is free if you do a certain number of trades a month  
  
cheers

  * [#56](/thread/post/2002661#post2002661 "Post Permalink")

  * May 16, 2008 12:16am  May 16, 2008 12:16am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Long position  
  
I enter in the last 10 secs of the entry candle with a nominal 10 pip tp and sl  
When im filled I modify my ticket to take tp at the top kelt band this is easy to do as the navigator window in MT gives you exact keltner price  
  
When I get a new 5min candle ,the keltners have obviously moved up or down and i simply modify the order again.  
  
If I'm in the trade for 20mins I enter once,then modify 3 times... 1 min before the end of each new 5min candle i get the modify ticket up and get ready to change it.  
  
This may seem like alot of hassle but it only happens once every 30mins or so  
  
paulus

Hi Zaka  
  
I took both of those   
  
Entry on the 1st I got 1.5442 I have a pain threshold of 15 pips and that got hit  
  
On the 2nd I got an entry of 1.5434 and was taken out at 1.5440 for 6 pips  
  
on both a 9 pip loss.. atm I cant see a way round it  
  
To put this in perspective since 9am ( the system was up 28 before that but i started at 9am today)  
  
Ive had 12 trades  
  
+17+11+26-9+16+15-9+11-7+11-15+6 = +73  
  
I enter then been placing stop 1 pip below low of entry bar for a long and 1pip above entry bar for a short..taking tgt in the same way and its been working very well...When i took the trade with the biggish loser I would have had to set a stop of 17 pips ...15 is my threshold.

  * May 16, 2008 4:04am  May 16, 2008 4:04am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi Ex  
  
the Bb can expand massively when volatility picks up the keltners tend to stay roughly parallel with price where as the BB can explode all over the place  
  
Unusable for this system as in alot of the case price would never move outside the bands  
  
paulus

  * [ ExpatXXXX](expatxxxx)

  * | Membership Revoked  | Joined Feb 2008 | [540 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=60281)

While I end my own trading day at 18:00 gmt, I lurk around a bit longer. I noticed your trade setup for a short at 1.5449. From my own observations, it seems prudent to check the Usd/Chf pair from the period of 18:00 to 20:00 as it seems to be another pair that works in an inverse direction to that of the Eur/Usd. Just another possible tool to help gage a trade in this pair. Do not mean to intercede, just an observation. A quick glance at the Usd/Chf 5m chart for the last hour or so will perhaps give some insight to my opinion.

  * [#84](/thread/post/2003114#post2003114 "Post Permalink")

  * May 16, 2008 4:33am  May 16, 2008 4:33am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Benq  
  
_Keltner_  
  
Length 10  
Times atr 1.0  
  
_Stoch_  
  
%K 15  
%D 3  
Slowing 2  
Low/high  
  
Only have signal line showing  
  
  
  
  
_Short_

  1. Close of candle above top keltner line and signal line on stoch above 80 
  2. Then I need a down bar with the signal line on stoch still above 80
  3. Enter

_Long _

  1. Close of candle below bottom keltner line and signal line on stoch below 20 
  2. Then I need an up bar with the signal line on stoch still below 20
  3. Enter

hope that helps  
  
paulus

  * [ jeta](jeta)

Look at asian session historically for EURUSD. [Spreads](/brokers/spreads "View Live Spreads on the Broker Guide") are usually small, the market is ranging, so over bought/over sold levels are respected higher % of the time than when the market is generally more trendy (which happens during European session and sometimes during US session).

From 9am to close system finished on 60 ( from open to 9am it gained 28) today I didn't get all that..88 in total I didn't get any where near all that as I didn't take all the signals...  
  
I havnt got a super filter it was just family life and the phone made it impossible.  
  
I still advocate taking 20-30 and running ..  
  
the biggest winner was around 26pips today not bad for a scalping system that throws out 30 odd signals but please be aware the losers have a max of 15 pips but average out around 7-8.  
  
This system will have losers any system will,but this is a mechanical system pure and simple..its easy to work with and easy to identify signals ....once your in you will have to modify your order ticket at the start of a new 5min bar to set the new tp at the K lines move.  
  
Paulus

Exactly. I think many people following this forum are sick and tired of people claiming their systems work, but after wasting many days of perfecting trading the strategy discover that the founder of the strategy actually loses money.  
  
Just check out all the systems on collective2.com. There is only _ONE_ forex system there that is somewhat profitable with a long track record. Not a good sign huh?  
  
Just look at all the damn threads on FF. There are THOUSANDS of them. After wasting an incredible amount of time, I have discovered that there are no more than 5-6 threads worth anything. The rest of the threads are started by newbies or losers that have come up with something out of a book and look for attention and followers and encouragement on FF.  
  
You have lagging indicators, bad risk/reward, no straight rules, slippage, and big spread all against you and you still claim you can do it? That's crazy! Show results.  
  
Real/Demo whatever, just show proof that it works.

Hi Paulas,  
I have just found this thread and have loaded up your template and gone over your rules, but I have a couple of questions, sorry if they are newb in nature ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

If I recall you said you wait until the last 10 seconds of the entry bar to place your order? So you set a nominal 10 pt SL and TP when you enter, then 10 seconds or so later you go back and adjust your SL and TP?  
The TP level you set is at the highest Kelt bar? Over a period of how many bars, or just the point it's at directly above the entry bar?  
Then you adjust your TP on every bar close? If yes then I assume it is indeed at the top Kelt bar above the new bar.

I also noticed on some post you had stated TP of 20-30 pips, which method is testing out better?  
Thanks, and sorry for so many questions, hopefully I won't have too many more once I demo test this for longer.

Hi All,  
  
Thanks for the posts my wife is fine thankyou.  
  
  
Hmmm not a good day by the looks it seems this system is going to need work to be profitable on Forex.This system was lifted over from Futures without any adaptation.  
  
Zaka see what your saying with your 3 entry play perhaps you can keep and eye on it and let me know how it pans out in the next week.Id be very interested as I think this system shows very good merit  
  
Aelimian yes you are correct although i think that will have to be changed.  
  
Pipsforall Expats system has been tried and tested over several months my system although great on Futures for the same period looks like it needs some filters judging by today,from the posts Ive seen Expat seems a calm and very controled inividual and would be a great mentor for any trader to follow and emulate.  
  
thehenryfam it seems i have to change a few things lols ..no back testing at all I traded the system on Futures for several months with very good returns.  
  
Tazman If I go short its in the last 10 secs of the bar I have the stop and tgt set to the approx levels of 1pip above the high of the entry bar and the level of the bottom keltner line.  
  
After im filled I click on modify ticket and adjust the SL and TP to the exact pips at the time of the entry bar ..each candle is 5mins so we have time  
  
then a new 5 min bar starts I leave the stop where it is ( 1 pip above entry bar) but as the bottom K line would of moved I adjust the TP with the modify order again.. Im working on refinments now

  * [#130](/thread/post/2006693#post2006693 "Post Permalink")

  * May 19, 2008 4:02am  May 19, 2008 4:02am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi Ex  
  
Initially on Futures I wanted to lock in $500 per contract and on the volatility at the time it seemed feasible.  
  
By using 2 contracts I increased my chances of doing it by closing 1 contract for +2 bringing the stop to break even on the 2nd..  
  
One more point of movement gave me +3 on my 2nd and $500 for the pair of contracts.  
  
The stop was set to 1point on each contract so a losing signal gave me -2 while a winning signal gave me +5 a nice risk return.  
  
With the volatility on Futures dropping I adjusted my targets to +1 and +2 giving me $300 for a successful signal against -$200 for a losing signal RR still positive so was happy  
  
As an example If I had the following +1+0,+1+2 ........after 2 trades Im sitting on +4 ( $400) when i take my 3rd trade because Im trading 2 contracts I would close when im 5 ticks in profit ( $50 per contract) this gives me 1 full point and 5 points for the day.  
  
I wouldn't wait for the normal 1 and 2 point targets to be hit.  
  
Money management would require you to go from 2 to 4 to 6 to 8 etc with each pair being trade giving you $500  
  
I think this approach has merit if it would work for you I couldn't tell.  
  
This is one advantage of having an EA for your system you could easily prog the stop scenario in and take at look at how it compares to your existing set up  
  
Hope that helps  
  
cheers  
  
paulus

  * May 19, 2008 4:39pm  May 19, 2008 4:39pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

Taz  
  
taking your suggestion of entering on the following bar but on a lmt order,my concern was that the really good signals just go and you would miss the entry.  
  
However on the signals above taking a lmt order with a view of covering the 2 pip spread   
  
ie if going long at 12 ( close of bar 10) then enter a lmt buy at 10..you gain 2 pips on every winner and save 2 pips on every loser ( with a fixed stop)  
  
On the trades above you would have +9-5 ( next signal didn't retrace so no +5) +6+14 =+24points  
  
I will look at this today  
  
cheers  
  
paul

  * May 19, 2008 11:25pm  May 19, 2008 11:25pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi FX  
  
I wasn't actually using the stoch to trigger the trades in the 1st lot of posts..I was using the stoch purely to show an OB or OS situation once I had that I was going short on the next down or up candle candle which worked extremely well on futures and got me in sooner as I wasnt waiting for the stoch to turn.  
  
This fix involves using the stoch in a more conventional manner and it needs to be quick hence the setting of 532 Im using it now to instigate the trade once outside of the top or bottom K line.  
  
This is obviously the standard way to use a stochastic but im not using main line going through signal to trigger ..will post at the end of the day if it seems to be working well.  
  
System on 42 I think a good cut off point for the day is 30 pip which is equal to my +2+1 = +$300 per contract on Futures  
  
cheers  
  
Paulus

Taz

  * [ tazmaan](tazmaan)

  * | Joined May 2008  | Status: Trader | [1,114 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=68173)

Paulus,  
No apologies necessary, as I am sure it's not you confusing me, just that I get confused ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1)  
  
For clarification, the way I look at your system is that we have a signal bar, and an entry bar. I think that's how I laid it out for myself. The signal bar is the one that closes under the bottom kelt, and under 20 stoch.  
The entry bar is the bar we wait until the last 10 seconds to see if it's an UP bar, then enter our trade right before it closes.  
With that in mind, since you said the bar you normally enter on, I assume you mean the entry bar, so you are letting it close completely, then taking 2 pips off it's close price and placing your trade at that limit.  
Hopefully this time I will understand it ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1) (and again, not your fault)

  * [#151](/thread/post/2008426#post2008426 "Post Permalink")

  * May 20, 2008 2:14am  May 20, 2008 2:14am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi Pippy  
  
Can i post a chart tonight just as a conclusion of things with the new entry criteria ?  
  
All what was happening was that taz suggested that rather than enter the market when you get a signal it may be a good idea to set a lmt order for the next bar as he noticed most signals retraced a few pips.  
  
So if my normal entry candle for a long finishes at 12 then set a lmt order for 10 on the next bar If price comes down to 10 we are filled for the long and 2 pips better off.Its a bit tricky to do you just had to be in the zone lols when the 5min entry bar finishes.  
  
The system I posted charts for on Friday used the stochastic just to show over bought over sold areas..if the stochastic went over sold ie below 20 then I would go long on the next up bar and would not look at what the stoch was doing..this is aggressive trading and gets you in sooner on the move and worked very well on US futures..  
  
Today I am looking at what the stoch is doing once we are outside the upper or lower K line and its in over bought or over sold area.  
  
I wont post now as I don't want to waste people time as it may not work long term ..   
  
But will post a chart tonight with how I'm looking at the stoch I hope you don't mind   
  
Paulus

Expat  
  
I used to trade Russell 2000 futures Er2 ..  
  
1 tick = $10  
1 full point $100  
  
Along with Dow Jones Futures,Dax Futures, and a little of the German Bund Future  
  
bid ask spread on Er2 was 1 tick so very tight and good to trade not sure about Euro Futures..from what I can see you need a future with a tight spread.

  * [#158](/thread/post/2008641#post2008641 "Post Permalink")

  * May 20, 2008 4:40am  May 20, 2008 4:40am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

ok still at suck it and see stage but looks promising your the experts any 'try this advice' will be wellcome the more the merier  
  
Im still using 20 and 80 for over bought over sold  
  
On my chart you will see   
  
Main line - white  
Signal line Red  
  
What i want to see for a long is   
  
Main line ticking up on the bar that is up  
the signal line must be going up as well but it need not have been below the OB or OS lines all i want is joint confirmation of UP or DOWN  
  
For a long If the main line is going up and the signal line is not it tells me we could be moving down more  
  
Ive labeled the signals to make it a bit easier  
  
A - uptick on main but signal down still and down bar - no sig  
B - Uptick on main down still on signal ( close but checked in navigator) - no sig  
c - up tick on both with up bar - sig - +7 pips + 9pips on lmt buy   
D - Down tick on main but signal up still - no sig  
E - Down tick on both with down bar - sig +6 pips +8 with lmt sell  
F - Up tick on main but signal down - no sig  
  
These are just a few examples were all in this game together so if you see a better solution just post it here,if you think something other than a stoch will work let me know  
  
im happy with this and will check on it throughout the week ..  
  
Ok got me tin hat on for incoming but 'waking the deads on tonight' and im a fan so be patient with me   
  
Paulus  
  
here is my template  
  
bugger I took all the arrows off before I saved my template so it would be clean for u guys and didnt take a screen shot arghhhhhh give me some time the chart will follow

  * [#166](/thread/post/2008843#post2008843 "Post Permalink")

  * May 20, 2008 7:33am  May 20, 2008 7:33am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi Bobcat  
  
Stoch below 20 price comes down through bottom band and closes below bottom band,I then wait for the stoch to up tick with price signal and main lines and i go long  
  
There are instances of stoch up ticking and price giving doji then doji then up bar..the system as yet is not hard and fast and that part of it is up to you.  
  
But for me I need the up tick of stoch and the up bar for the long entry all to happen at once .. By sticking to this approach im trying to reduce signals firing off in the opposite direction when a strong trend develops.  
  
The main line will tick more often than not with price but in strong trend the signal line keep going with the trend and so stops you taking a signal  
  
It doesn't stop them all but it helps..I'm more than willing to change the settings or add another confirmation indicator or another type of filter if some one recommends them  
  
The system is there to be used and abused broken and remade .. with the outcome being a logical well tested system  
  
paulus

I added the attached indicator: Center of Gravity ( I got this from another thread in this forum).  
  
If this indicator is added to Paulus strategy, I found that the success rate will be more. The COG indicator too is not fixed It changes position and is a lagging indicator. But this helps.   
  
I take a long trade when the price touches the bottom line of Keltner band, the bottom green line of COG indicator and when the stochaistic is below 20.  
  
For short Vice-versa. I fell that the success rate is more when we add COG indicator.

For people visiting the thread its all gone quite mainly due to the fact Im still working on perfecting the entry.It gives good signals and think Ive cracked the signal against a trend problem ..just looking at the stop..either move to break even when we hit the middle ma line OR take the stop 1 pip above high of bar for a short and 1 pip below low of bar for a long..  
  
Or like i use it on Futures ( trading 2 contracts or always in pairs)when i make 1 full point I close and move stop to break even on 2nd ....then close 2nd at +3 giving me 3 full points per pair of contracts traded ,3 full points on ER2 futures is $300  
  
Still experimenting  
  
Paulus

  * [#174](/thread/post/2013095#post2013095 "Post Permalink")

  * May 22, 2008 2:50am  May 22, 2008 2:50am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Ive been trading for most of the day missed out the real early period flat at mo..but have had 11 signals got 9 of them .. system on +57 pips  
  
been taking lmt buy and sells all day only missed 1 signal due to the fact the signal didnt retrace to hit my lmt buy,.  
  
I find the process easy I get the order ticket up and select pending order and set stop and tp to roughly the right levels..   
  
I then wait for 2-3 secs till the end of the 5min candle and click on one of the arrows in the 'at price' box this gives me as close as possible the close of the candle and then click submit and the order gets filled..waiting to get hit  
  
This way I gain 2 pips on the tp as on a long I get in 2 pips lower than the close of the bar so the spread is covered and as my stop is fixed..if long I set stop to 1 pip below low of entry candle so my loss is 2 pips smaller also.  
  
the missed signal was 7 pips but have gained 2 pips on the other 10 so one way or another am 20pips up less the 7 on the signal that didnt get triggered, so 13 pips better off so far for using the lmt buy and sell  
  
Using 2 x stoch one is standard 532 the other the Stoch DiNapoli set to 833  
  
Will post final results tonight with my template ..  
  
The Keltner moves forward in it evolution  
  
Actual trades +4+3-6+7+13-4+15+12-5+11+7 = +57  
  
Flat now waiting for a short   
  
Paulus

Hi BenQ  
  
Yes thats right if long tgt set to top K line if short set to bottom K line.  
  
seems to work well if you long and the price is rolling over and it looks like its going to move against you the top K line comes down to meet your fill and you get taken out albeit for a smaller amount but it saves you in a way if it rolls over slowly  
  
Er2 really good I like it tried YM alot of my friends trade it but never got on with ES is moves in a strange way..  
  
the good thing about US futures is that the dep required to trade is so low now so its a good return for your money  
  
Paulus

yes thats correct..other wise taking it to the extreme you could have a series of doji candles with stoch coming down from OB into OS and then get a down bar...you cant go short ..  
  
it has to happen with stoch ticking down at same time as candle is a down candle all happening from above the 80 line..ie bar before signal is above 80 then down tick with down candle..thats your signal  
  
Paulus

Hi Benq  
  
I only use that stoch to help eliminate a few signals,its the fast top stoch that helps with entry.  
  
by saying 'it takes no further part' just means that by the time it goes OB or OS its done its job for me in determining a signal or not..I dont watch it again untill the next signal..it has no input into the entry that all done by the faster top stoch  
  
BUT ...... as you know I'm completely open to suggestions  
  
Cheers

  * [#195](/thread/post/2017802#post2017802 "Post Permalink")

  * May 24, 2008 5:15am  May 24, 2008 5:15am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Thanks cC  
  
No I havnt looked at other time frames,once i get the 5min firing on all cylinders I'l look at a few other time frames for those longer term bigger gains..  
  
Thanks for posting the chart   
  
Ive had a good result today on the K system ....  
  
Rules i used today in the trading room   
  
Longs  
  
_signal in normal way  
  
_

  1. Price closes below bottom K line
  2. Stoch Di below 30
  3. Stoch normal below 20
  4. Stoch normal ticks up at the same time as an up bar

_Entry_

  1. Set a lmt buy 2 pips below the close of the signal candle
  2. Wait to get taken
  3. Fix the stop 1 pip below the low of the entry candle
  4. Set target is 10 pips

The fixed target worked well today ,even in trends as Im going counter trend the 10 pip tgt has a chance of getting hit.With a fixed stop if we enter with a lmt buy 2 pips below the close we are in effect getting in minus the spread and reducing our potential loss by 2 ticks  
  
We are also increasing the chances of getting out with our target.  
  
The draw back is the move can happen with out price coming down to your lmt buy.  
  
_Example  
_  
Signal at 10  
Set lmt buy at 08  
Low of bar 04 set stop to 03 ( stop is 08 - 03 = 5 pips)  
target 10 pips so set at 18   
  
Without lmt buy but entering with mkt order  
  
Signal at 10  
mkt entry at 12  
Low of bar 04 set stop to 03 ( stop is 12 - 03 = 9pips)  
target 10 pips so set at 22  
  
Signals today  
  
-2+10+9+10+10+10-8+10+10-7-5+5+10-7-7+10 ( not filled not counted) -2+1+10 = +57  
  
Cheers Paulus  
  
ps daily tgt of 30 pips hit early in the day

  * [#200](/thread/post/2018081#post2018081 "Post Permalink")

  * May 24, 2008 7:26pm  May 24, 2008 7:26pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Hi All  
  
We may of fixed the K trading system its taken 10 days or so but it now looks very promising.  
  
I will post my template and the Stoch Di with this post also  
  
SIGNAL LONG

  1. Price closes below bottom K line
  2. Stoch Di below 30
  3. Stoch normal below 20
  4. Stoch normal ticks up at the same time as an up bar

_Entry_

  1. Set a lmt buy 2 pips below the close of the signal candle
  2. Wait for the lmt buy to get filled
  3. Fix the stop 1 pip below the low of the entry candle
  4. Set target is 10 pips

RULE

  1. Once we have our lmt buy order placed we wait for price to come down to our set lmt.As long as the calculated target has not been hit we leave this order open
  2. To make things clearer if the close of the candle is 10 we set our lmt buy to 8 our prospective target is 18 as long as price hasn't hit 18 we leave our lmt buy open
  3. If the target of 18 ( example above) is hit and we havnt been filled on our lmt buy of 8 yet then at that point we cancel our order and start looking for another signal
  4. If we get a signal in the opposite direction whilst in a trade we reverse

The figures below are all signals generated and are manually back tested ,I live traded several ...as no EA is available the manual back test was the only option open to me.  
  
The signals are taken from the whole session 0.00 to to 0.00 Monday 19th up to Friday 23rd   
  
  
  
Monday  
+10-2-2+10+10+10+10-5-3+10+10+10-11+10+10+10 =+87 pips  
  
Tuesday  
-3-1+10+10+10-8+10-7-6+10+10+10+10+10+10-5+10+10-2+10 = +88 pips  
  
Wednesday  
+10-3+10-2+10+10+10-8-5-5+10-4+10+10 = +54  
  
Thursday  
+10-4-3+10-3+10-7-7+10-5-5+10-4+10-2+10 = +30  
  
Friday  
-4+10+10-6+10-3+10-4-9+10+10-2+10+10+10 = +62  
  
Im very happy with the above results esp the loser/winner ratio in terms of hits and size..it gives a fairly good risk return.This is done by taking the lmt buy and sell to reduce the losing trades and exit the winning trades quicker  
  
A target of 30 pips a day is achievable I think and seems to be a good cut off point...no point in sitting in front of the pc all day !   
  
A couple of signals a day were not taken as the lmt order was not hit before the signal hit its target so a potential 20 pips on average per day is missed by these trades but is outweighed I think by the tighter stops.  
  
The chart I have posted shows a 'messy' signal to show you how the lmt buy order works there are other signals on the chart but not marked some winners some losers.  
  
I have also included an example of your ticket once you are filled on the lmt price you can go into your account management and click on 'modify ticket' to adjust stop and tp to the exact pip   
  
[http://www.turboimagehost.com/p/3522...20/%3E%3C/a%3E](http://www.turboimagehost.com/p/352214/eurusd_example.gif.html%22%20target=%22_blank%22%3E%3Cimg%20src=%22http://s2d1.turboimagehost.com/t/352214_eurusd_example.gif%22%20border=%220%22%20alt=%22Free%20Image%20Hosting%22%20/%3E%3C/a%3E)

>  I will post my template and the Stoch Di with this post also  
>    
>  SIGNAL LONG
> 
>   1. Price closes below bottom K line
>   2. Stoch Di below 30
>   3. Stoch normal below 20
>   4. Stoch normal ticks up at the same time as an up bar
> 

> 
> _Entry_
> 
>   1. Set a lmt buy 2 pips below the close of the signal candle
>   2. Wait for the lmt buy to get filled
>   3. Fix the stop 1 pip below the low of the entry candle
>   4. Set target is 10 pips
> 

> 
> RULE
> 
>   1. Once we have our lmt buy order placed we wait for price to come down to our set lmt.As long as the calculated target has not been hit we leave this order open
>   2. To make things clearer if the close of the candle is 10 we set our lmt buy to 8 our prospective target is 18 as long as price hasn't hit 18 we leave our lmt buy open
>   3. If the target of 18 ( example above) is hit and we havnt been filled on our lmt buy of 8 yet then at that point we cancel our order and start looking for another signal
>   4. If we get a signal in the opposite direction whilst in a trade we reverse
> 

> 
> The figures below are all signals generated and are manually back tested ,I live traded several ...as no EA is available the manual back test was the only option open to me.  
>    
>  The signals are taken from the whole session 0.00 to to 0.00 Monday 19th up to Friday 23rd   
>    
>    
>    
>  Monday  
>  +10-2-2+10+10+10+10-5-3+10+10+10-11+10+10+10 =+87 pips  
>    
>  Tuesday  
>  -3-1+10+10+10-8+10-7-6+10+10+10+10+10+10-5+10+10-2+10 = +88 pips  
>    
>  Wednesday  
>  +10-3+10-2+10+10+10-8-5-5+10-4+10+10 = +54  
>    
>  Thursday  
>  +10-4-3+10-3+10-7-7+10-5-5+10-4+10-2+10 = +30  
>    
>  Friday  
>  -4+10+10-6+10-3+10-4-9+10+10-2+10+10+10 = +62  
>    
>  Im very happy with the above results esp the loser/winner ratio in terms of hits and size..it gives a fairly good risk return.This is done by taking the lmt buy and sell to reduce the losing trades and exit the winning trades quicker  
>    
>  A target of 30 pips a day is achievable I think and seems to be a good cut off point...no point in sitting in front of the pc all day !   
>    
>  A couple of signals a day were not taken as the lmt order was not hit before the signal hit its target so a potential 20 pips on average per day is missed by these trades but is outweighed I think by the tighter stops.  
>    
>  The chart I have posted shows a 'messy' signal to show you how the lmt buy order works there are other signals on the chart but not marked some winners some losers.  
>    
>  I have also included an example of your ticket once you are filled on the lmt price you can go into your account management and click on 'modify ticket' to adjust stop and tp to the exact pip   
>    
>  [http://www.turboimagehost.com/p/3522...20/%3E%3C/a%3E](http://www.turboimagehost.com/p/352214/eurusd_example.gif.html%22%20target=%22_blank%22%3E%3Cimg%20src=%22http://s2d1.turboimagehost.com/t/352214_eurusd_example.gif%22%20border=%220%22%20alt=%22Free%20Image%20Hosting%22%20/%3E%3C/a%3E)
> 
> Ignored

Thanks so much Paulus!!!![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f647-200d-2642-fe0f.png?v=15.1)

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Harar  
  
Hi  
  
We have to have a tick up on the top stoch as thats the faster of the 2 with an up bar..the lower stock 90% of the time follows suite but as long as its below its 30line im happy to carry on with the trade  
  
Its a traffic light effect... we need 4 green lights  
  
green light - price closes below bottom K line  
green light - fast ( top ) stoch below 20  
green light - stoch Di below 30  
green light - top stoch ticks up with price  
  
I get the ticket up with 10 -20 secs to go and as soon as i see we are ending the bar I click 'place'  
  
Then go to modify ticket and adjust tp and stop to exact pips  
  
Hope that makes sense  
  
cheers  
paul

  * [#207](/thread/post/2018209#post2018209 "Post Permalink")

  * May 24, 2008 11:17pm  May 24, 2008 11:17pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

I must stress though to those that scan this great forum..you will have losing trades on this method.  
  
I dont know of any one any where who doesn't have losing trades  
  
And in all the statistics on any system there will be lurking the 6 losers on the trot the big losing days..  
  
On the flip side the stats are also in there for the 6 winners in a row and the really big winning day.  
  
Please please no matter what system you are using don't bin it because you have a bad day look at it and try to find out what went wrong.  
  
This may not be the full and final version of the K system I dont know one thing I do know the the less we expose ourselves to the market the better for our risk... get your 20 or 30 or what ever fig you want to put on it and close down for the day.  
  
Look at it this way you start at 8am the markets great the moves are excellent 3 trades and 3 x 10 pips.. you stop at 30..You exposure has stopped you no longer risk the losing runs the quiter times.  
  
If Im on 27 pips for the day and my next signal moves 3 pips I close it and bank the 30 for my money managment  
  
If I posted a system here that made a 10 pip loss every day on a back test for the last 365 days it wouldn't get 1 post and no interest..but If I posted that it ends up with a 10 pip loss but at some time during the days on each of the last 365 days it was up by 40pips at some time it would get alot of interest ..   
  
I always look at what its done during the session rather than whats its done at the end of the day  
  
Im not preaching just letting you know how my mind works  
  
I done allot of research into this when i traded Dax futures I worked out hope much per hour i was making if i stopped at a certain points value each day...It showed back then I would earn more per hour stopping at a certain value than if I traded the whole session.  
  
Rather than post the link I have copied the actual post dated 25-1-2003 from a BB called Technical Traders of which Im a moderator  
  
_**End of week totals week 1**_  
Dax = £17 per point   
_**Scan A**_  
Stopping at +3 = 140points in 24.5 hours of trading = 5.7 points per hour   
All day = 160 points in 55 hours of trading = 2.9 points per hour   
Strike rate up to +3 = 63%   
_**Scan B**_  
Stopping at +3 = 140points in 21.5 hours of trading = 6.5 points per hour   
All day = 260 points in 55 hours trading = 4.7 points per hour   
Strike rate up to +3= 62%  
  
If time is off an issue and the thought of sitting in front of the pc for 11 hours is daunting then the above shows that to stop at +3 winners over losers is the way to go.   
Look how low the points per hour dropped to when trading the whole session.Agreed more money would of been made if you traded the whole sesion,but at a far slower rate.One of my aims I hope to achieve with my trading apart from financial independance and security for my children is the freeing up of far more leisure time.I do not intend to give up the day job just to sit in front of a PC screen 11 hours a day.   
  
Both scans avergaged around the same time for +3 wins 21-23 hours per week.  
  
_**Putting this into financial gains(+3)**_  
Scan A and Scan B achieved the same 140 points or £2,380 not inc costs for 1 contract in 23 hours max for last week.   
_**Costs were as follows (+3)**_   
Scan A 41 trades = $230 around £139   
Scan B 56 trades = $313 around £189   
  
Ok its only 1 week but the result make my pursuit of this seemingly worth while.   
Will keep you up to date with any developments   
Paulus

Hi,  
I just realized this other one has a bunch of extra features.  
Paulus: now you can also watch TV downstairs and leave the baby monitor on (as you can do with Futures), this one has sound alerts, as well as email alerts (someone said he worked with internet access but couldn't stand all day in front of the monitor?)  
The color blocks is also useful, you don't want to be "staring" at the screen all day long, you can be anywhere in the room and have this big blocks telling you if you must be paying attention or can continue reading.  
This is also by Mladen.  
Hope it helps.

  * [ tazmaan](tazmaan)

  * | Joined May 2008  | Status: Trader | [1,114 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=68173)

Hey Paulas,  
Back from vacation, and it looks like you have made some nice changes to the system. Trying to get all caught up on things and just had some clarifications.  
  
I will post my template and the Stoch Di with this post also  
  
SIGNAL LONG

  1. Price closes below bottom K line
  2. Stoch Di below 30
  3. Stoch normal below 20
  4. Stoch normal ticks up at the same time as an up bar

_Entry_

  1. Set a lmt buy 2 pips below the close of the signal candle
  2. Wait for the lmt buy to get filled
  3. Fix the stop 1 pip below the low of the entry candle
  4. Set target is 10 pips

Are we still waiting for the close of the next bar to be an up bar and using that as our signal bar (with which we are taking 2 pips reverse of the close as entry price)?  
Or are we just waiting for an up tick on the bar, and an uptick on the stoch at the same time, no matter how much time the bar has left etc?  
Been playing around with it this evening a little bit but this part has me a little confused. Seems the successful way to get into a trade and not just be completely passed by, is to have an up bar in the last 10 seconds or so, use the current market price in that last 10 seconds of the bar to subtract 2 pips from for our entry price. Then 10 seconds later after it closes, we use the low of the bar as our stop, and add 10 pips to our entry price as our target?  
Could be way off as usual, please enlighten me ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)  
Hope you had a good holiday as well. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#232](/thread/post/2027253#post2027253 "Post Permalink")

  * May 30, 2008 7:49am  May 30, 2008 7:49am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar14698_3.gif) jagui](jagui)

  * | Joined Jul 2006  | Status: Trader | [281 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=14698)

This basically is a "revert to the mean" system, and is a **good one**.  
It will work great when there is no trend in place, and it will fail when there is a trend in the traded timeframe, because it will try counter-trend entries.  
What should be really added to this system is a trend filter: just trade it when there's no trend. When trending, trade another system. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

Hi Batoobah  
  
That was a good valid set up but looking at the bar and taking the n2 pips lmt you sould of only lost 2-3 pips on that signal with a tgt of 10 it gives us quite a good risk return.  
  
Im still on hols so havnt got time to nswer all the questions posted but if you set a lmt buy 2 pips below the close of the signal bar and set your stop 1 pip below the of the signal bar your losses will be kept to a min  
  
Or if you prefer you can set your stop to _break even when the price touches the middle average K line_..that will save aquite a few but may also mean you will miss out on some good winners.  
  
Was there not a nice short signal 16 bars from the left on your screen shot that may of gone for 10 pips ? you would of got filled on the lmt sell around 4-5 bars after the signal bar  
  
sorry have to run   
Cheers  
  
Paulus

  * Jun 5, 2008 11:18pm  Jun 5, 2008 11:18pm 

  * [ cChris](cchris)

  * | Joined Jan 2008  | Status: Trader | [45 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=58168)

Hi X,   
  
Put the indicators into the "experts/indicators" folder where you installed MT4, for example under "Interbank FX Trader 4".  
  
Put the template into the "templates" folder where you installed MT4, for example "Interbank FX Trader 4/templates".  
  
Restart your MT4 and then load the template. If you want to combine them with your indicators, don't use the template but pull the indicators on your chart individually to add them to yours.  
  
Hope this helps! Chris

  * [#247](/thread/post/2042082#post2042082 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 7, 2008 6:47am  Jun 7, 2008 6:47am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

The fix saved me having several losses today so here it is  
  
Hi all  
  
Back off hols and thanks for the posts..I love the coloured Stoch makes things very easy on the eye. Do you think there is a chance of doing it with the DiNapoli Stoch....just a thought  
  
ok this may be a fix for the trend problem. One day last week it saved 40 pips of loss by keeping you out of most of the tending periods. It will cut out a few winners but overall it should save more.  
  
If you put an RSI set to 14 on your chart, and look at just the peaks we are not interested if it is above or below OB or OS..this technic is an offshoot of some thing that was taught on the Trader International course which I took 4-5 years ago.  
  
Its just simple diversity  
  
The chart below shows how to use the RSI and how to work out what peaks to use.  
  
The RSI is only used when we have signal in the same direction..so if we had short short short short short then we would use the RSI as a filter as these may be firing off in a trend against our signals.  
  
If we have Short long short long then we don’t use and the sequence is broken by a signal in the opposite direction  
  
Sooooooo  
  
Long long ( use) short (no need) short (use) short(use) long (no need) etc etc.  
  
Hopefully the chart below will explain better  
  
I have used a white dotted vertical line to show where the RSI peaks are they will always be 1 bar behind the actual signal bar  
  
As you can see the 1st long we take as it’s the 1st since the one before off the chart was a short.  
  
  
1st signal – We take  
2nd signal – If you look at the RSI peak we made a higher high so we leave  
3rd signal – Again we made a HH on the RSI so we leave  
4th signal – We can take as the RSI peak made a lower low  
  
I must stress this will also stop you taking you some winners but I think stopping the losers is more important. If you had 6 wins and 6 losers for the day and applying this technique cut that down to just 2 wins for the day then we have achieved our aim.  
  
Again the system is ongoing and this I suspect is not the full and final version.  
  
  
  
Paulus

When applying your template to the chart, only Dinapoli stochastic appears. Do you use mainly Dinapoli stoc or classic stoc for validation of the signals?  
  
Thanks for this nice system  
  

> [Quoting Paulus](/thread/post/2042082#post2042082 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> The fix saved me having several losses today so here it is  
>    
>  Hi all  
>    
>  Back off hols and thanks for the posts..I love the coloured Stoch makes things very easy on the eye. Do you think there is a chance of doing it with the DiNapoli Stoch....just a thought  
>    
>  ok this may be a fix for the trend problem. One day last week it saved 40 pips of loss by keeping you out of most of the tending periods. It will cut out a few winners but overall it should save more.  
>    
>  If you put an RSI set to 14 on your chart, and look at just the peaks we are not interested if it is above or below OB or OS..this technic is an offshoot of some thing that was taught on the Trader International course which I took 4-5 years ago.  
>    
>  Its just simple diversity  
>    
>  The chart below shows how to use the RSI and how to work out what peaks to use.  
>    
>  The RSI is only used when we have signal in the same direction..so if we had short short short short short then we would use the RSI as a filter as these may be firing off in a trend against our signals.  
>    
>  If we have Short long short long then we don’t use and the sequence is broken by a signal in the opposite direction  
>    
>  Sooooooo  
>    
>  Long long ( use) short (no need) short (use) short(use) long (no need) etc etc.  
>    
>  Hopefully the chart below will explain better  
>    
>  I have used a white dotted vertical line to show where the RSI peaks are they will always be 1 bar behind the actual signal bar  
>    
>  As you can see the 1st long we take as it’s the 1st since the one before off the chart was a short.  
>    
>    
>  1st signal – We take  
>  2nd signal – If you look at the RSI peak we made a higher high so we leave  
>  3rd signal – Again we made a HH on the RSI so we leave  
>  4th signal – We can take as the RSI peak made a lower low  
>    
>  I must stress this will also stop you taking you some winners but I think stopping the losers is more important. If you had 6 wins and 6 losers for the day and applying this technique cut that down to just 2 wins for the day then we have achieved our aim.  
>    
>  Again the system is ongoing and this I suspect is not the full and final version.  
>    
>    
>    
>  Paulus
> 
> Ignored

Put every thing apart from the template in your   
  
MetaTrader -experts - indicators folder   
  
Put the template in your   
  
MetaTrader - templates folder  
  
If you have MT open..shut it and reopen...you should now find the template in your template tab and the rest listed in the inds tab under custom  
  
BUT if have put every thing where it should be..you need only load the template as it will find for itself what it needs  
  
Paulus

Paulus...  
  
Concerning the peaks of the RSI, on the image it looks like   
you are measuring the RSI peaks from Signal to Signal,   
and not from the most recent "previous" RSI peak to   
the most current RSI peak, right?  
  
In other words, are you concerned with the RSI peaks  
only from the _previous_ RSI peak nearest the _previous_ Signal...  
and then "measuring" to the most _current_ Signal and it's  
associated _current_ RSI peak?  
  
I hope my question is clear.

  * [ peej](peej)

  * | Joined Jun 2008  | Status: Trader | [4 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=71733)

Greetings Paulus and all, This is my first post to forex factory. I have read this thread from start to finish and tried this method on demo today. Very nice work. I found myself missing many entries because I was simply doing other things. To show my appreciation for this thread I have modified the Keltner channel code to include a simple alert when either of 2 conditions are met: (1) price close > upper keltner AND stoch >= 80 (2) price close < lower keltner AND stoch <= 20  
  
I hope this proves useful and you can tell me if there are any issues. I find that some good entries are missed because 80/20 may be too stringent but they can be adjusted. Also this code is not very far off from being a very simple EA.  
  
Here is complete list of changes:  
1) changed name to Keltner Channel Paulus mod02.mq4  
2) changed default Lenth = 10  
3) changed default TimesATR = 1.0  
4) changed default color to red  
5) added arguments for: Alerts_ON=true, StochKPeriod1=5, StochDPeriod1=3, StochSlowing1=2, Upper_Stoch_Threshold=80, Lower_Stoch_Threshold=20  
  
Things that could be added: email alert, ???  
  
\--peej

  * [#269](/thread/post/2049355#post2049355 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 11, 2008 9:59pm  Jun 11, 2008 9:59pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar12442_6.gif) hoss](hoss)

  * | Joined Jun 2006  | Status: Lifelong learning... | [774 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=12442)

This system has been working great for me with the original settings. The only thing that I added to it were auto pivots and the 60 ema (you may want to add the 200 also). What I look for patiently are set ups where the stoch is OB or OS, a closing outside of the KC, and confluence with a pivot or the ema that provides normally some resistance. I concentrate on one currency cross, EUR/USD. This does a few things. It keeps me focused on one currency, keeps my spread low, and forces me to take only the best set-ups. I also keep an eye on price action on the 30min and 4hr, but when you are scalping the 5min, normally they don't have an impact unless you hit a 4hr trend line. I am also willing to TP at the middle line in the KC. This is usually good for about 5 pips or so. I look to grab about 10 pips a day at higher leverage and have been consistent with it. I affirm to myself that I am a sniper and I will only shoot when I am very confident that I will hit. Patience pays. 

Attached Image

![](/attachment/image/120666?d=1213189166)

Life is too short to have anything but delusional notions about yourself.

  * [ davidwillis](davidwillis)

here is my first version of the the keltner ea. It still has some bugs, but I thought I would post it, since I am not going to have much time for a few days to work on it.  
  
Just as a note, this is in its early stages, so don't use it on a live account.  
  
Also I noticed that the colored stochastic set to 532 actually reads like a regular stochastic set to 533. So the ea is using a stochastic of 533 to match my colored stochastic on my template.  
  
Have fun with it, and let me know what it does wrong.  
  
David

You can't run two ea's on the same chart, but you can open another chart and put another ea on that chart. As long as they have a different magic number, they will not interfere with each other.

> 
> Interesting system. I trade a variable of the same. Trade only Eur/Usd on the 5m tf. Utilize Stochastic set at 5-3-3, ADX set at 4, a 2sma and 5 sma with a weighted close. Trade from 5 - 11 a.m. pst and average about 10 trades per session with good results (90%). Look to take three (3) pips of net profit and trade 8 contracts per trade. Has been very consistant and profitable for the past eight months. Currently indure a 2 pip spread and have had very little difficulty. Can obtain confirmation by dropping down to 1m tf to time entry and exit. Never trade during "red" news announcements. Thanks for sharing. Keith

The SL 1 means 1 pip past the signal candle.  
the limit amount is you set your limit order to. if it is one, it will enter the trade when it retraces 1 pip from the close of the signal candle.  
The start and stop times are based on your broker time.  
the slippage, is that the max you will allow your trade to be off. So if you enter long at 1.5570, you may get in at 1.5575 if the market moves really fast right when the order is sent.  
  
Sorry I didn't explain much of how it works. 

"No man is free who is not master of himself"

#  [](/thread/86476-5-min-keltner-system)5 Min Keltner System 

  * 

  * [#281](/thread/post/2050816#post2050816 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 12, 2008 1:19pm  Jun 12, 2008 1:19pm 

  * [ davidwillis](davidwillis)

  * | Commercial User  | Joined Mar 2005 | [386 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=1887)

It has been opening some, in fact the problem with it right now seems to be that it opens too many after a loosing trade.  
  
Remember that it uses more than just the k bands to signal a trade. You have the rsi filter, and the two different stochastic indicators. Then it also needs to retrace back to the limit level (default is 2 pips).  
  
I can't remember if I left all the all the comments in the one I posted, but if you don't have a bunch of information on the left had side of your chart, you can uncomment them.  
  
If you do have them, this is what they mean:  
  
Last signal bar - is the number of bars back to the last bar to signal a trade (stochastics are overbought or oversold, the bar before closed outside the k band)  
  
Second last signal - is the bars back to the signal bar before the last one  
  
Last signal direction- is the direction of the last signal bar (0=long, 1=short)  
  
second last signal direction- is the direction of the signal bar before the last one (if both are in the same direction, the rsi filter comes into play)  
  
pips moved - this is the max pips moved in the direction of the trade since the last signal bar (if this is past the tp level, it will not enter the trade on a retrace)  
  
rsi filter - 1 means it will enter a trade even if it is in the same direction as the last one, 0 means it will not.  
  
trading time - if it is 1 , it means your are in the time frame to be traded in (ie london, us, depending on your settings)  
  
last entry - this is the price it should enter on if it retraces back, if it does not retrace back to that point before it reaches it's take profit point, it will not enter a trade.  
  
last trade - the seconds since the last actual trade was entered with the same magic number and currency pair that the ea is on  
  
last sig - the seconds since the last signal bar  
  
  
Any way, I hope that is helpful.  
  
and yes, you need the indicators (I think the only one that is not already in metatrader is the k channel one) in your experts/indicators folder (and may need to restart your platform after copying them there) , but you don't need them on your chart. 

"No man is free who is not master of himself"

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar47020_2.gif) jacioux](jacioux)

  * | Joined Aug 2007  | Status: Trader | [99 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=47020)

I have been reading over this system and i feel that it has a lot to offer. When looking it over i noticed (attached chart) the when Stoch are in either over bought or over sold right before it heads down the current candle is inside the previous candel. Not sure if anyone else picked up on this but it seems to move about 10 pip (where you enter) up or down. maybe insted of using RSI as a guide and keeping you in or out of trades perhaps this one bar inside the previous bar could be the signal. Looking it over for the past month i see a few examples where it headed up or down and reversed but if you put your stop at 1 pip above the previous bar you are only losing about 4-6 pip. Just thought i would add my 2 cents to this system and maybe help out a little.

Just a note and observation about this method. I think it provides excellent entry clues for other methods such as fibs and S&R trading. For example, if you do a fib of thursdays range a nice short entry was provided at the 50% retracement fib on friday at about 1:15am GMT (2nd red arrow). If you would have held this order for the duration of the fib move your looking at 150+ pips in your account.

Watching this EA for the last couple days, I think I am noticing it not placing trades when it should, or placing them late.  
However someone should verify the rules, as I am not positive I am up to date on them.  
Once the close is above keltner and above both stoch's, the next bar is ticking down. Isn't the order placed during the last 10 seconds of the down bar? The EA seems to place it into the next bar, not sure why. That is when it places the trade at all, I think since open tonight I have seen 2 triggers but EA didn't place any trades.  
Of course I could be missing something, as I still don't quite understand the RSI or I have the wrong RSI settings, as to me it looks pretty much like a flat line with very little movement. Maybe my RSI settings are wrong.  
Anyhow, will continue to watch and monitor the EA, hopefully other's are doing the same?

  * [#307](/thread/post/2056852#post2056852 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 16, 2008 12:27pm  Jun 16, 2008 12:27pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar47020_2.gif) jacioux](jacioux)

  * | Joined Aug 2007  | Status: Trader | [99 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=47020)

Had a little time before i have to put my daughter to bed and here is what i traded. Starting with SUNDAY OPEN this is when the markets opened up 3pm  
MST -6GMT.   
A - here is the first signal as you can see we are over sold in STOCH and looking for the bounce up, BUT the candle after the bar inside DID NOT move  
up i did not take the trade, there were 2 signals BOTH did not move up.   
B - Stoch are heading down the small bar is inside the previous bar +10  
c - Stoch are heading down the small bar is inside the previous bar +10  
D - Stoch are heading up NOW this bar formed and the previous candle did nto move but if you look 2 bars ahead it did move up - DID NOT TRADE  
THIS  
E - Stoch heading down bar inside the previous bar +10  
F - THIS IS A VALID SIGNAL the durrent bar engulfed the previous bar and STOCH are heading up +10  
G - Stoch heading down bar indisde the previous bar + 10  
H - was the last signal before i typed this....and looking at it now it did go up +10  
+60 pips from 3pm to 9 pm (mountain standard time MST)  
For what ever reason when one bar is inside of another bar and we are over bought or over sold wait for the one pip move up to confirm direction  
and then enter trade. Again this might be beginners luck but that seems to be a very powerful signal and back testing over the past month i have only  
found a handful of times where the signl would move then revers but if you place your stop on the previous bar you are risking about 5 - 8 pips.   
Hope this helps some of you  
J

  * [#310](/thread/post/2057055#post2057055 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 16, 2008 4:05pm  Jun 16, 2008 4:05pm 

  * [ tazmaan](tazmaan)

  * | Joined May 2008  | Status: Trader | [1,114 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=68173)

David,  
Another EA observation (along with it not taking all the signals properly I think, as mentioned previously).  
The EA is taking a signal and behaving properly UNTIL the trade goes the wrong direction and stops out. At that point, instead of just taking the 6 pip loss and waiting for another signal, it is chasing it. As soon as it hits the stop, it instantly places a new order, with another 6 pip SL and the orignal TP level. I assume you did this on purpose but wasn't aware that was part of this trading system. Anyhow, in the case of 06:40 candle (fxdd time), this sucker just kept dropping like a bomb and the EA triggered 4 trades on this bar alone.  
I assume it did it for you as well so you are aware, but if you need more detail let me know.

Hi Jacioux,  
  
thanks for your observations. Do I summarize it correctly when you:  
\- take longs only after the bar following an inside bar breaks the inside bar to the upside  
\- take a short only after the bar following an inside bar breaks the inside bar to the downside  
\- apply both rules only when both price action is outside the Keltner bands (below it for going lon, above it for going short) and the STOCHs confirm direction.  
  
Would that be a correct summary of your findings?  
  
cheers  
Ohka

Hello Tazmaan,   
  
You are correct on the bounce down there.   
  
As for the band yes i do use them but i use them more for a comfirmation. Just to mention the bar inside does have a name its called a Harami (just learned that). So an example would be lets say i notice that the bars are getting closer to either the high or low band, i then wait for the Harami to form near that bar and then enter. I understand the system now wants the bar to be on the outside but i just noticed that when the Harami does form its close to the bars, and if it does form on the outside of the bands then the move has a lot more momentum with it. I also use the base system found on the first post of this system.   
  
My main point i want to point out is the formation of the bar before a move. Granted there are a lot of other valid signals and this system is just amazing i like to have more confirmation when i trade.

Ohka,   
  
That your summary is correct. But i also want to point out that i use the Keltner bands as a guide. If the Harami (bar inside) i wait for the Hatami to form only near the bands not inside them.   
  
If you go back to the first post whent he system is being described i use that as my templete and ONLY enter when Stoch are over bought or over sold. I NEVER enter even when the Harami forms and i DO NOT have the stoch in either postion. The base set up of this system is key i am only pointing out what the bars like to do before they make there move. I have only noticed this EUR/USD and the best time (i feel) to trade this is 10pm to 6 am (MST) that is about 6 hours behind GMT.   
  
thanks

fib and S/R notes - monday June 16  
  
My goal is to use the Paulus system for entries that i can keep going all day long. My bias was down today because trend is down until it changes right? Well it was down for a while but went up.  
  
(1) 61.8 fib of fridays range. Didn't stick.  
(2) 61.8 fib of fridays range. Stuck for a while.  
(3) Reversal. Gold and oil rising, 5350 Support (Euro seems to have support at all 00 and 50 levels), and 61.8 fib of up trend starting on Friday.  
(4) If you missed entry 3 then entry 4 was a nice break/retest of 61.8 level and it was a 38.2 retracement of the new uptrend and it was approx 5400 level support.  
  
I got trades 1,2, and 4. Missed 3 because my bias was down.  
\--peej  
  
Remember everybody, German ZEW tommorow

Thanks David,  
I have put it in place and will keep an eye out. As far as the candle timer issue, in the next update if you could just move your comment section down a couple of lines it might fix the problem? Worth a shot.  
  
I have already noticed what I think was a missed trade. I am not sure what rules you are using specifically tho. From what I follow, bar closes above keltner and above both stochs, it's a valid signal. Next bar must be a down bar and in the last 10 seconds of the bar we place a sell order.  
I am not sure if this is what you are doing, but if so, the candle that just closed a trade wasn't placed (interbank time 05:05 is the signal, 05:10 should have been the entry bar).  
I'll watch out for our chasing issue in the meantime.  
Keep up the good work!! ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

> Ignored

That is strange, because I am trading this on my alpari demo, and it got that trade.  
  
Anyway, this is how I understand what is needed to enter a trade (Paulus can correct me if I have it wrong![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)). Here is an example of a short trade:  
  
1- A close above the kelter channel with the stoch above 80 and the denapoli stoch above 70  
  
2- A down bar that also moves the stoch down  
  
3- The last signal needs to be a long trade, or the rsi peak to peak is sloping down  
  
4- The price needs to then retrace the limit amount before it reaches the Take profit level to enter the trade.  
  
P.S.   
  
Paulus, I just read on the X's thread that you had to take your daughter for an emergency operation. I hope all is well. 

"No man is free who is not master of himself"

The rsi only comes into play on two consecutive trades in the same direction. As long as you have a long, short, long, etc.. you don't use the rsi (at least according to the system).

Results for 6/17 with latest EA  
10 trades   
6 wins  
4 losses  
+32 pips  
  
I still believe there are more trades to be had, however I am still not quite getting the RSI situation, as for the most part mine shows up as a straight line pretty much, not many peaks to speak of.  
  
David, in your EA, is it easily changeable to change the following?  
a. not use the RSI at all for confirmation  
b. place the order in the last 10 seconds of the bar (or even at close if that's easier to program) at market, instead of the 2 pips back or whatever it's using now.  
  
I think these are the only two things I am noticing less trades being taken between these two methods, and wouldn't mind running a backtest and forward test to see which method results in the best gains.  
  
Great job on this btw, wish this thread were more active, would love to see other people verifying the EA's trades and helping fine tune this thing to perfection.  
Maybe some interest will develop here soon.

  * [#333](/thread/post/2061210#post2061210 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 18, 2008 12:50pm  Jun 18, 2008 12:50pm 

  * [ tazmaan](tazmaan)

  * | Joined May 2008  | Status: Trader | [1,114 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=68173)

Yep, you've done it correctly. As long as you have all the required indicators as well, it should trade (RSI, the two stoch's and the keltner bands). Make sure the keltner band indicator name matches the name in the EA settings.  
If it doesn't trade for awhile and you see that it should be based on what david's trade rules are, check the start time and end time settings as well in the EA.  
Glad to have you on board the test ship!

Thanks for testing, and the feedback.  
  
p.s. your rsi should look like the one I attached. It helps to uncheck the maximum and minimum setting on the rsi, so you can see the peaks better.

  * Jun 19, 2008 6:57am  Jun 19, 2008 6:57am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar56490_3.gif) Paulus](paulus)

  * Joined Dec 2007 | Status: Trader | [2,600 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=56490)

Ok been gone a few days  
  
RSI works well to a degree but try this approach..its nothing new  
  
use your 5min chart as normal but ignore RSI ( stop crying your grown men lols)  
  
Open a 15min chart with same template,if you want remove the price bars...we want the inds  
  
We get a normal short signal on the 5min..take a look at the 15min stoch was it over sold is it now going down..in my case was it green is it now heading down from OS   
  
2 charts 1 is all the signals today so far..the 2nd is an example 5 and 15min time stamped at 9.30pm..the white +figures are the nornal 10 pip tp..the yellow is closing the 5min signal when the 15min stoch goes OS for the short OB for the long  
  
In my futures trading software I could easily write a scan to look at the 15min whilst on the 5 min..it would give me a green bar on the bottom of my chart..if green go with 5min sig if red leave easy peasy lemon squeezy  
  
Paulus

Hi Steve..  
  
the long signal was where the arrow is we do have a down bar followed by an up bar but the stoch did not tick up at that point it was flat ..we then had the down bar then on the upbar with the arrow the stoch ticked up..confirmed by 15min   
  
The next signal (9.20) although it was later ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) the 15min stoch was heading down so not go for the 5min  
  
And well done on the 11.10 signal I missed that and it did win and was confirmed by the 15min..  
  
havnt abandoned the use of the RSI looking at other possibilities to reduce loses and increase the success rate of the signals left.  
  
When i brought this system over from Futures it was a completed system..but on Forex it was only 50% efficient..its only through the posts here that the system has been adapted and improved for Forex use..  
  
Hope all that helps  
  
paulus

Thanks Paulus,  
  
I see what you mean by that trade, i didn't realise that you would take an entry when the initial signal and entry was not valid. In this case, a further signal and entry bar confirmed and you took it, even though this second down bar was not outside the keltner band. In this case, all that was wrong with the first signal was the stoch not ticking up so the second one meant it was good to take.  
Hope your family recover soon.  
  
Cheers,  
Steve  
  
ps David has written an EA, has anyone tried to backtest these rules with Strategy Builder or something to see how it fairs in the past? Seeing as this is a mechanical approach, there seems no reason why this cannot be done?
